FNV PBR PPLIGHTING RESOLVER TEXTURE-DATA VTABLE FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Follow resolver slot +0x0C output below E90B10 into source +0x24 renderer-data.
2. Identify constructor/factory vtables for source-texture renderer data and returned wrappers.
3. Decompile slots +0x98/+0x9C/+0xA4/+0xA8/+0xAC/+0xB4 before assigning material-map semantics.
